\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Matroska file demuxer \begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Ronald Bultje \href{mailto:rbultje@ronald.bitfreak.net}{\texttt{ rbultje@ronald.\+bitfreak.\+net}} 

with a little help from Moritz Bunkus \href{mailto:moritz@bunkus.org}{\texttt{ moritz@bunkus.\+org}} 

totally reworked by Aurelien Jacobs \href{mailto:aurel@gnuage.org}{\texttt{ aurel@gnuage.\+org}} 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
specs \mbox{\hyperlink{filter__design_8txt_ae1f616347c13c08d2255bb22a3263fe4}{available}} \mbox{\hyperlink{writing__filters_8txt_a95df7a7ff85fb8f73f62d3c5d2d325f8}{on}} the Matroska \mbox{\hyperlink{vsrc__gradients_8c_ac03d07aecfcb4992ad8ccb38f9eb3e39}{project}} page\+: \href{http://www.matroska.org/}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+matroska.\+org/}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
